enforcement and out-of-order/out-of-bounds sample detection through several coordinated mechanisms:\\n\\n## Series Creation and Lifecycle\\nWhen appending samples, if a series doesn't exist, it is created through the `getOrCreateWithOptionalID()` method in `tsdb/head.go` (line 1844). This method invokes a `SeriesLifecycleCallback.PreCreation()` hook (line 1845), which can return an error to prevent series creation. This allows external implementations to enforce cardinality limits.
